!-   ===========  ALL OBJECTS IN CLASS: ZONEHVAC:IDEALLOADSAIRSYSTEM ===========

! Air system do pavimento terreo
ZoneHVAC:IdealLoadsAirSystem,
    te_canto_11_sala Ideal Loads Air System,  !- Name
    sch_hvac_sala,           !- Availability Schedule Name
    te_canto_11_sala Ideal Loads Supply Inlet,  !- Zone Supply Air Node Name
    ,                        !- Zone Exhaust Air Node Name
    ,                        !- System Inlet Air Node Name
    50,                      !- Maximum Heating Supply Air Temperature {C}
    13,                      !- Minimum Cooling Supply Air Temperature {C}
    0.0156,                  !- Maximum Heating Supply Air Humidity Ratio {kgWater/kgDryAir}
    0.0077,                  !- Minimum Cooling Supply Air Humidity Ratio {kgWater/kgDryAir}
    NoLimit,                 !- Heating Limit
